Flowerbomb was created by Olivier Polge, Carlos Benaïm, Domitille Michalon Bertier and Dominique Ropion. Top notes are Tea, Bergamot and Osmanthus; middle notes are Orchid, Jasmine, Rose, Freesia and African Orange Flower; base notes are Patchouli, Musk and Vanilla. This perfume is the winner of award <b>FiFi Award Best National Advertising Campaign / Print 2006</b>.</p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>An explosive bouquet of fresh and sweet notes arrives with perfume Flowerbomb, designed by Olivier Polge, Carlos Benaim and Domitille Berthier.</p>

<p>It was introduced in 2005, as an oriental perfume. </p>

<p>Top notes tingle with fresh and sweet accords of bergamot and green tea.</p>

<p>A heart is floral and opulent with intensive, sweet and pure Sambac jasmine, seductive Centifolia rose, freesia and Cattleya orchid. Musk and patchouli in a base wrap us with an oriental scent, while its milky and powdery notes gently fondle our skin.</p>

<p></p>

<p>The bottle was designed by Fabien Baron, in shape of diamond-granate, alluding at the fragrance itself, since it is so explosive, sophisticated and glamorous. It was introduced at the 10th anniversary of Viktor&amp;Rolf house’s work. It is available as 30, 50 and 100 ml EDP and EDT.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" style="font-size: smaller; color: #83a6c4">Read about this perfume in other languages: <a It smells floral, sweet, and delicious. Girly, sexy, playful, youthful, fun. Don’t get me wrong this is not juvenile though. You could wear this from the office to a club to a restaurant to a date to a funeral to a church to a grocery store. Do you get what I’m saying. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1784272">kittenpawz</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-15">10/15/24 11:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>You can downvote negative comments and sing praises all you want but it won't stop this damn near solinote patchouli monstrosity from being an insult to the art of perfumery. I once made the mistake of spraying the tiniest bit in the kitchen with the purpose of disguising the reek of onions and for two whole days it smelled like multiple flower pots have been broken in there. Dirty smell overall, even more skanky on a person when the musk comes out to play. If you're olfactory sensitive, don't approach this, it's headache in a bottle. All flowerbombs have that stomach-turning quality native to the whole line, and the only thing that varies from flanker to flanker is the degree of vileness. The original, however, is potentially the worst perfume ever made. There's not an ounce of femininity in it, and it's as sweet as musty soil.<br />
<br />
Edit: okay well not the worst ever if you spray just once and violently rub it into your skin. But then performance suffers and it smells like any other minty grape soda celebrity perfume. I want so badly to find something, anything appealing about it since I had wasted a whole gift card on it but it's beyond me. Maybe when it's finally discontinued and I shamelessly sell my 30ml for $5k I'll be able to spare it some love but for now I stand by what I said.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2182719">marianaavilal</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-09">10/09/24 11:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I've worn this for years and it's one of my favorites, but one of my favorite experiences with it it's that it's transformed with the years. When I first got it (maybe 6 years ago?) it was a candy floral, well, bomb. Sweet, girly, juvenile but not childish. It was a bright and happy scent for spring and summer days. I bought it in Disney World and it always made me picture a theme park day.<br />
<br />
With time it has become more prominent on the patchouli, tea and musk to me. It has transformed into a cozy rainy fall day scent. And I LOVE that. I no longer think it's juvenile, it makes me feel clean, put together. It's a scent I love to put on to stay home and read, to drink a cup of tea. It's still sweet and floral for sure, just more grounded, skin-like, and mature as time goes on. Feels like it's grown with me.<br />
<br />
Edit: For clarification, I still have my same 6-year-old bottle. The juice is quite dark now. This isn't a matter of me perceiving a perfume differently, the juice has literally changed with time. So, don't expect the second paragraph's description to apply to a brand new bottle!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2310139"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2310139#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2305160" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This fragrance is a more mature version of the same scent, which I very much enjoy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2294567"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2294567#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2294533" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2294533" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="aratarei"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2266003"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2266003.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="aratarei" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Miss-Dior-Blooming-Bouquet-2023-78945.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.78945.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Miss Dior Blooming Bouquet (2023)"title="Miss Dior Blooming Bouquet (2023)"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2294533ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2294533" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2266003">aratarei</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-25">09/25/24 07:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So, I was at this cozy little café downtown, the kind where you can sip your coffee while people-watching. I was sitting there, minding my own business, when a woman walked by and left a trail of the most enchanting scent behind her. I mean, I literally turned my head to see what it was! It was this beautiful floral aroma that was bright yet had depth. Naturally, I had to know what she was wearing.<br />
<br />
After a little chat, she told me it was Flowerbomb by Viktor &amp; Rolf. I made a mental note because I knew I had to check it out. Fast forward a few weeks later, and I finally treated myself to a bottle. I was excited, especially since I love floral scents, but I also lean towards the fresh and fruity side rather than anything too sweet or heavy.<br />
<br />
The first time I sprayed it, I was hit with an explosion of flowers—like I had just walked into a blooming garden. The bergamot in the top notes was refreshing, and there was this beautiful mix of jasmine and orange that felt really uplifting. I loved how it wasn’t just a straightforward floral; there was something more complex underneath.<br />
<br />
But here’s where things got a little tricky for me. As it dried down, I started noticing that patchouli note. At first, it was okay, but after a while, it became a bit too prominent for my taste. I’m not the biggest fan of patchouli, and while I appreciate how it can add depth, it started feeling a little overpowering. Some reviews mentioned it smelling a bit “old lady,” and I could see where they were coming from.<br />
<br />
Another thing that surprised me was the longevity. I expected this scent to stick around all day, but I found myself needing to reapply after just a few hours. It was kind of disappointing because I loved how it made me feel initially, but I wanted that feeling to last longer.<br />
<br />
Despite these quirks, I could see why so many people rave about it. It definitely has a unique personality, and I think it would shine in cooler months or for special occasions. If you're looking for something to wear on a night out or a date, it definitely gives off that confident vibe.<br />
<br />
In the end, I’d give Flowerbomb a solid 6.5/10. It has a gorgeous opening and a lot of character, but the patchouli and lack of staying power just didn’t vibe with me as much as I hoped. I think if you love rich, complex florals, this might be right up your alley, but for my everyday wear, I’ll probably stick with lighter, fresher options.<br />
<br />
So, while I’m glad I tried it and enjoyed those initial spritzes, I think I’ll be passing this one along to a friend who might appreciate it more than I did!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2258968">kerropii</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-23">09/23/24 08:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>**I am new to the fragrance world I don't have the best most informative reviews, I go based on vibes**<br />
<br />
This is a very interesting and in my opinion unique floral fragrance, It is floral fragrance but instead of it turning sweet it has this background of patchouli and tea almost turning it into a very very faint light smokiness to it. It feels very POP, yet has that twinge of greenery to it that I really enjoy!<br />
<br />
I would not recommend this to anyone who is looking for a pure floral or a floral/sweet scent because of the kinda greenery happening in this fragrance. I find this to be better in the colder months, spring would be okay too. Not a summer time fragrance but perfect for all day or all night <br />
<br />
Very nice projection and longevity in my experience my only complaint is I almost immediately have a sense of nose-blindness to it, I wind up over spraying, than experiencing a headache from it later. I wish I could avoid that with this fragrance but it's very hard too, which makes my experience wearing this fragrance not as pleasant to wear for me sadly.<br />
<br />
If you have migraine/headache issues, I would not recommend this because this type of scent can induce it or make it worse. <br />
<br />
Overall, a 7.5/10 (points taken off because it's prone to giving me a headache)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2292451"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2292451#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2290137" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1269119">fairymeist</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-07">09/07/24 20:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>What took me soo long to get this perfume?<br />
<br />
 Thanks to my most recent purchase ( Cheirosa 76 - previously After Hours by Sol de Janeiro) I found out it apparently smelled identical to this perfume, I fell in love with the new Cheirosa so I blind bought Flowerbomb without ever trying it before. And yes! It smells just like the new Cheirosa scent, now I have a perfume which I can pair with the mist. <br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2207357" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="dear_jax"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2179680"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="dear_jax" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2207357ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2207357" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2179680">dear_jax</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-03">07/03/24 14:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I received a decant of this perfume to try out since I owned Cabotine Fleur Splendide, and that EDT has been compared to this. I have also seen comparisons to the OG La Vie Est Belle, a fragrance I found too saccharine. Still, I wanted to try it out.<br />
<br />
On me, Flowerbomb pulls very sweet, like cotton candy as others have noted, and quite floral with the jasmine and rose being noticeable. I also get some patchouli, which I am not a fan of, although it does cut the sweetness a tad. While not a bad scent by any means, this perfume feels a bit linear to me. Cabotine seems to be more fruity overall and quite woody in the drydown, which I prefer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2207357"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2207357#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2203395" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Slightly more interesting than La Vie Est Belle; less interesting than Angel, with whom both of them share a lot of DNA.<br />
<br />
Of course, you WILL smell good wearing this. It smells like cotton candy and patchouli; what could be bad? It is simple, cute and easy to wear. Probably the biggest mark against it — and this is true of the whole fragrance family — is that an awful lot of other people will smell like you.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It’s very sweet, vibing heavily with what we might know culturally as traditional cis femininity. I pick up much more on  the sweet notes with the florals as an afterthought, sort of like the stage upon which a singer performs. They’re there, but not the star of the show. Mainly, I wanted to review this scent because a lot of articles name it as a longevity beast that will get noticed, &amp; I didn’t find it to be that. Summer maybe pushing it a bit for this but it’s a good office scent and not offensive. Extremely feminine.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2168322"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2168322#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2163030" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The liquid is orange instead of pink now. But it still smells nice.<br />
On first spray it's very strong. I could smell the bergamot, which had a sort of alcohol-ish tinge.<br />
One hour in it's not as strong. I sprayed it on my wrists, and I can't smell it unless I put it up to my nose. But when I do the smell is still fragrant. The alcohol smell has faded and while bergamot is still mostly what I'm getting, the florals are becoming more prominent.<br />
Three hours in it's definitely faded a lot. Most of the top notes are gone and it smells distinctly of florals.<br />
More than 8 hours in and I can smell the base notes very well. Vanilla is the strongest. <br />
Overall feminine standard perfume. It's not exactly what I want to smell like but it smells good. Longevity is great, lasted far longer than I expected for one spray rubbed on both wrists. Sillage was intimate, but I imagine it might be stronger if I had sprayed more on different places.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2158862"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2158862#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2158854" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I loved it back then, of course. It was a hyper-sweet aphrodisiac to me, and it walked a fine line between girly-girl and woman. Now it's overplayed, like sugar-beast Angel that came before it - everyone wore it. But I still appreciate it. Flowerbomb is iconic in its own right. <br />
<br />
In all honesty, I can't differentiate the notes from the sweetness. The tea note gently shines through, but otherwise it's liquid floral sugar and should have been named Sugarbomb, lol. <br />
Overall it's pleasant and beautiful, with big projection and average longevity.<br />
<br />
La Vie est Belle shares a very similar DNA. If you own one, you don't need the other (unless you just like collecting, of course.)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2144763"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2144763#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2141899" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I decided to give it another chance after a year, because it was the only perfume I had left. Now the bottle is almost finished and I'm considering buying it for myself this time. <br />
If you want a classic feminine and sexy scent that is not suffocating, then this is it.<br />
However, I have to say that it doesn't last very long. In the first 2-3 hours I can smell it just fine, but after that it fades away pretty quickly. In my experience, the projection is intimate to maybe moderate and sillage is almost non-existent, but that is to my liking. <br />
So far, I've gotten one compliment by a friend who said I smelled really nice after we hugged. My grandma is usually annoyed by perfume, but when I sprayed this, she said the room smelled like actual flowers.<br />
Overall, it's a yes from me and I'd go as far as to say it's a safe blind buy.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2137760"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2137760#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2133064" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1900683">heliotrope317</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-22">04/22/24 16:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Shhh, this is one of my most favorite scents as though it were made for me. It blends into glory on my skin so much so that I have bought 4 bottles so far.  Now that has never happened before and some can't even believe that it's Flowerbomb that I am wearing.  I receive compliments on it wherever I go, people getting close to me to sniff for no reason. Dark spicey, creamy smooth, not too sweet, from the open of the sambac jasmine and rose down to the holding of the patchouli and vanilla end.  Until I find my ultimate creamy sandalwood dream perfume, this one will stay close to my heart.  This is not a sweet lipstick scent, rather it is pure spicey delish scent that haunts.  I think that everyone has magical perfume notes that are special for them and I hope that you one day find yours.  Oh I will buy this one again, and again, and again, and again.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2133064"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2133064#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2128557" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1691326">summervanilla</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-02">04/02/24 06:47</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I did not like this scent for a really long time. I don't even remember why and what my impression of it was. I smelled it when I wasn't very knowledgeable about fragrance, then avoided it as I learned more because I thought I disliked it. I tried it once or twice and it didn't agree with my body chemistry and my nose at all. It gave me a headache and didn't smell nice on my skin. But I still had the sample, and I have been trying to use up all my samples, so I gave it another try. I don't know why, but suddenly I kind of like it. It smells really sweet on my skin. I would agree with everybody who says it isn't very floral. It's like flowers drenched in honey and covered in sugar. I get the similarities with La Vie Est Belle, but they aren't quite the same. Maybe Flowerbomb is her sister, I can't say who is older and more mature. I realize now that I have a few random, cheap perfumes that are dupes or clones of Flowerbomb. While I find I suddenly like this fragrance, I do like the dupes I have better for one reason or another. This would probably be a safe blind buy despite my experience. It would make a really good first fragrance for a young lady or anybody who is interested in sweet, feminine leaning fragrances.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2022848">slmbrkty</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-13">03/13/24 10:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A decent, easy to wear, non-offensive floral. I enjoy the scent, but Flowerbomb feels the same as so many other floral fragrances for a way higher price tag. I do not personally find anything profound about this scent or formula. The tea, rose, and jasmine are prominent upon first application, and then it settles into a nice spring day with a blanket of musk underneath. Longevity and sillage are moderate-high; lasts about 4 hours on my skin, a little longer on clothes, and it has a nice sillage that radiates just enough from the body. I would give it a 6.5/10, maybe a 7.5 if the price point was lower. I don't hate this, but I am not head over heels for Flowerbomb. I do not plan on purchasing a full bottle, but it's a good fragrance to keep a vial of when you're in the mood for it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2091427"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2091427#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2090642" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1945520">lavieenrose1987</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-12">03/12/24 16:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>As I’m still new on my fragrance journey, I asked a more knowledgeable acquaintance for recommendations. After listing off a few currently popular choices and some niche fragrances, she then giggled and said, “or, if you want to be basic millennial, you can get Flowerbomb.” Honestly, that right there confirmed that I needed to get my hands on at least a sample. <br />
<br />
While I get that the fragrance industry is just as bad as fast fashion when it comes to a constant stream of new releases and trends, things that are labelled “basic” are popular for a reason. This is a smooth blend of floral and patchouli with some spice on top which gives it a unique kick. I’m not big into super girly and photorealistic florals, so this is a fantastic alternative for someone who wants something feminine with a twist. It’s a fragrance that resonates better with women in my opinion, so if that matters to you, this is your girl.<br />
<br />
If this is what qualifies as “basic”, then call me basic. I notice that Baccarat Rouge 540 is already falling from grace into that category, so don’t worry. Whatever your current it girl fragrance is, it and you will be framed as “basic” soon enough, then "grandma" in a couple decades from now. I look forward to the day that “basic” and “grandma” stop being used as descriptors for scents that have historic popularity.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2090642"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2090642#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2090227" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2090227" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="risarii"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/71405"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.71405.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="risarii" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Lattafa-Perfumes/Yara-76880.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.76880.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Yara"title="Yara"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2090227ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2090227" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/71405">risarii</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-12">03/12/24 09:43</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I avoided this fragrance for a long time because of its annoying popularity, as I think a lot of people did. Now that it’s seemingly less ubiquitous (despite being sold at Sephora, I guess many girls have moved onto Black Opium which now seems to be the ubiquitous it girl) I decided to smell it. And I must say, it was quite good. Very good, even. Possibly great but I’ll wait to say that until I smell it again. <br />
<br />
I think the tea and osmanthus keeps it from being too generic gourmand/fruitchouli (a la LVEB). It’s well-composed, high quality and sort of hyper feminine (though maybe I’m just being influenced by the adorable bottle). I never thought I’d want to own a bottle but here I am, considering buying a bottle. <br />
<br />
Excellent throw and longevity.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2090227"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2090227#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2089718" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2083499" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="yukikiki"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1527214"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1527214.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="yukikiki" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2083499ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2083499" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1527214">yukikiki</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-05">03/05/24 17:45</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A sweet, floral, tea fragrance. The patchouli is present but not overwhelming. It's extremely well blended and I can't pick out where the sweetness might be coming from except maybe the vanilla orchid. Nowadays not groundbreaking but beautiful nonetheless. <br />
<br />
Have not smelled anything similar to it, and disagree with the votes in the "reminds me of" section that it's similar to LVEB. LVEB is more lipsticky and more iris based.<br />
<br />
I'm not sure if it's weak or if I go noseblind to it, but it seems to become faint rather quickly. I don't love this fragrance since I don't gravitate towards tea notes, so I don't think I'll repurchase a full bottle. But I will have a travel spray around. I've never smelled it back in the day and have no scent memories or nostalgia attached to the scent. It also doesn't smell outdated. <br />
<br />
Not work appropriate in my opinion. But great for a signature, date nights, and day to day wear. Too sweet for summer imo.<br />
<br />
Wonderfully made fragrance. Worth sampling.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2083499"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2083499#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2082525" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I was perusing the perfumes at a Zara in El Salvador, and Black Peony struck me. It was a little dark and fruity, warm and sensual and maybe a touch loud (although keep in mind, I was wearing it in blistering heat with no air conditioning). I kept the bottle for years and eventually it went rancid.<br />
Now I'm testing Flowerbomb, and there's just something about it that smells so...right. I didn't know it back in the early 2000s, so I don't have those "dear God, it's everywhere" associations. To me, it smells like--hear me out--lilac-colored chocolate. Not lilacs, but the color lilac and soft chocolaty nuances. I know I'm not the only person who struggles to describe a perfume that really touches them, but that's what I get. In absolutely the best way. It blends into my skin, easy on the nose. I may just be a typical 2000s girl, but I love it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2082525"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2082525#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2080851" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I don't think it's anything really groundbreaking nowadays but it's really a safe, soft, sweet floral creamy fragance. Very feminine. I especially like the patchouli and sweet, flowery, warm vanilla in this.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2080851"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2080851#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2076830" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2067937" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Maya lilac"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1705079"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1705079.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Maya lilac" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2067937ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2067937" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1705079">Maya lilac</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-20">02/20/24 03:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Flowerbomb was a love of mine since the end of 2000’s when it was released. I remember smelling it back in the days and feeling mind blown, no exaggeration… At some point in my life, all I wanted to wear was Flowerbomb and La Vie est Belle. These two were my favourite perfumes for about a decade…<br />
<br />
Flowerbomb is a very feminine, sensual, big bouquet of flowers, sweet vanilla based that  has a prominent patchouli note. What made this particular scent so appealing to my nose was the juxtaposition of green tea, osmanthus and patchouli. I still love it very much! It does something to me in a way that I can’t explain…<br />
<br />
I like that it’s an airy, clean, sweet floral, with fresh citruses on top but also has a strong, warm, heavy base to counterbalance the composition. It’s so well done and so addictive and lasts for days on clothing. Performance on Flowerbomb was never a issue, it’s freaking fantastic!! Creates a nice scent bubble around me that makes me feel pretty and happy…<br />
<br />
 I went through  two big bottle back in the days, and I bought a third one a few years ago. While I still love it when I wear it, I noticed that I don’t reach for it so much. I feel like even though it not so unique to smell anymore because it is so popular, the scent itself is still unique! <br />
<br />
I will always have Flowerbomb in my collection, it’s a cult classic now. This scent is one of my first perfumes, and one of those who made me fall in love with perfume (and also with the note of patchouli).<br />
<br />
Iconic scent that aged well, unlike La Vie est Belle…</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2067937"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2067937#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2063135" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1993630">Amamii</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-29">01/29/24 18:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Every time I see Flowerbomb, it takes me back to 2014. At the dazzling perfume counter, I was immediately drawn to this bottle shaped like a pink hand grenade (although it was quite an eye-catching one). The design and appearance captivated me. After sampling the fragrance, it felt like bustling flower market, yet the scent was comforting and not overwhelming in the slightest.<br />
Its top notes are a very fresh floral scent, dominated by rose and osmanthus, with a subtle hint of tea aroma; the middle notes also blend floral scents, feeling softer than the top notes. However, these are not the scents of flowers in a vase, but rather of fresh flowers planted in the soil or at least in flower pots, giving me the impression of vibrant, lively flowers.<br />
Since then, I've tried many perfumes with various floral scents, but I've never encountered another fragrance like this one. It's not an aquatic floral scent, but rather a warm floral one, likely brought by musk and vanilla. Typically, the combination of flowers and vanilla could be too sweet for me, and I don't particularly enjoy this mix in other perfumes. However, it came to my realization after using fragrance with patchouli as base note, that it was patchouli note that toned down the sweetness.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I’m more of a gourmand lover. This is a floral one all the way, so if you love florals it’s for you. It’s very warm, it has nice projection and good longevity. It’s a sexy smell but definitely not my favorite. I would give this a 6.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2043878"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2043878#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2040512" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It helps that it has really good lasting power and sillage, so for daily wear one spray is totally sufficient. In fact, my dad is the one who gifted it to me originally, and he generally complains that I was too liberal with application if I use two sprays, so I only ever do so for going out in the evening.<br />
<br />
That said, as much as I used to love this scent, my perception of it has changed over the years. Something about the strong patchouli combined with the bergamot has started feeling caustic to me, almost scraping at the back of my throat. A lot of people describe this perfume as delightfully fruity, floral, and warm, and I know for a fact that I used to feel the same way, but for the past couple of years all I've been able to smell is patchouli bomb, haha. While I don’t know if I’d purchase a full size, or more precisely a full price full size, I’ve been having fun with my rollerball. I quite like the patchouli hard candy vibe other reviewers have pointed out. It makes me feel like a very pretty, sweet girl with a significant other who dotes on her, a close knit group of friends, and who is always organized and on top of things (but maybe that’s just me projecting my wishes onto the scent). It’s been beloved by so many for a reason. <br />
<br />
I do find it irritating how many reviews seem to be not only calling the scent basic but insulting its wearers. It’s true Flowerbomb has mass market appeal and has been so prevalent in the fragrance world since its release that it now seems not only basic but more than a little passè to many fragheads. But mass market appeal is nothing to scoff at and this is the inevitable journey any highly popular fragrance will pass through. Glossier you, Santal 33, Baccarat rouge 540, Delina etc are starting this transition as well, and soon will be similarly scoffed at. Finally, all that making snide comments about the type of individual that wears this scent or similar others do, is make one look like someone who is into perfume for the exclusivity, rather than sincere appreciation of the art.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2019363" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Shimmer412"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1889185"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1889185.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Shimmer412" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Kayali-Fragrances/The-Wedding-Silk-Santal-36-83208.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.83208.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="The Wedding Silk Santal | 36"title="The Wedding Silk Santal | 36"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2019363ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2019363" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1889185">Shimmer412</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-03">01/03/24 17:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>So, I’m not typically drawn to many floral fragrances, but the Flowerbomb line (OG, Ruby Orchid, Nectar, and Midnight) is absolutely beautiful! I also am very careful about fragrances that have patchouli notes because if not done right I don’t like them, but again I think Flowerbomb (as well as the flankers) are all done right!<br />
<br />
Flowerbomb is a softly sweet floral that’s flirty and romantic! I don’t get that mature scent that I find with a lot of florals which might be why I love this one! I also don’t find the rose note to be very forward, so that’s probably part of it too! While I do notice the patchouli I also don’t find it overpowering, rather more grounding and enhancing of the other notes! I really love the orchid, orange flower, jasmine, vanilla, musk, and even the patchouli notes in this! <br />
<br />
For reference a few other florals (besides the Flowerbomb flankers) that I really love are Coach Love (2012 version), Chloe Love Story, Chloe, Coach Poppy Blossom, Coach Poppy Wild Flower, JPG Classique, Kayali Deja Vu White Flower, and Nest Golden Nectar! I have noticed that I do tend to like amber florals and Solar florals. I don’t know if these are exactly considered strictly florals, but also Dolce &amp; Gabbana The One and Sol de Janeiro 59.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2019363"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2019363#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2017784" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I dare not wear it yet. I may be biased but I don't think anybody can pull it off quite like she does. <br />
<br />
This really is a flower bomb, it fills the air with floral prettiness. I think it is neither especially youthful or especially mature, it's very timeless and elegant. I think Anya Taylor-Joy was a great pick for the ad campaign. The warm spicy notes twinkle and dance on top of the florals.<br />
<br />
It's heavy, too. It seems to last forever. When my mother leaves the house, the bathroom still smells like Flowerbomb. It's quite a pleasant way to fill the space.<br />
<br />
I imagine: ballerinas sipping champagne after a great opening night, Grace Kelly in pale pink satin, an evening stroll in the garden, and Cinderella's ball.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It’s a feminine, sweet and fresh floral with a little hint of vanilla later on. <br />
I’ve been wearing this consistently for the last 10 years. I never get bored of it and it’s one of those rare scents that suits all occasions and seasons. <br />
<br />
I don’t think it’s an explosion of floral like the name suggests though, it’s obviously floral but has a freshness to it.<br />
I love the fresh green tea, orange, freesia and patchouli. <br />
It’s a very well composed perfume that lasts all day on me ( even longer on clothes) <br />
<br />
I don’t care that it’s ‘over’ popular (although, I hardly smell it in anyone nowadays)  <br />
A good perfume is a good perfume🤷🏻♀️<br />
<br />
It’s also the scent I’m guaranteed to get compliments on, my sister bought a bottle after smelling it on me &amp; my mum is always saying ‘oooo you smell nice’ when she hugs me &amp; im wearing this.<br />
<br />
I can’t say I fully get the LVEB comparison. <br />
LVEB smells sweeter to me, I really like it but prefer Flowerbomb.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2005938"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2005938#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2005009" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Neither is it a heavy patchouli that smells like your local metaphysical shop. The two notes are both extremely powerful within this perfume, creating a scent that reminds me a lot of floral pastries. The patchouli smells more like a doughy vanilla scent when combined with the floral notes, which are themselves slightly diluted by the base notes. This is still an overwhelmingly powerful perfume, and will stick to your clothes for days after. You are best off walking through this scent rather than spraying it on directly. I imagine the woman who owns this perfume would regularly wear it to springtime afternoon teas.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="1988838"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=1988838#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1985457" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; And you’ve grabbed some sugar cookie biscuits to have along with it. The combo is a 3 pm tea time well suited for cooler weather (perhaps not a dead of winter type). If you have both I highly recommend mixing them to breathe new life into V&amp;Rfb.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="1974952"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=1974952#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1972581" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1882005">cutiepi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-02">11/02/23 21:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Seeing all the great reviews I decided to give this one a go. I sprayed it on a tester card and liked the scent, so I sprayed it on myself to see how it would wear. <br />
<br />
This smells terrible, there is something incredibly bitter and rank about it I just didn't like. After about 4 hours it has dried down a bit so it's not as awful, and I can smell some more floral coming through, but this one is still a no for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="1967273"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=1967273#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1965763" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1965763" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="WhiteFlowerPrincess"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1662712"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1662712.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="WhiteFlowerPrincess" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Lucky-48385.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.48385.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Lucky"title="Lucky"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1965763ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1965763" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1662712">WhiteFlowerPrincess</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-11-01">11/01/23 05:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don't mind this fragrance, but it still leaves a lot to be desired and is quite generic smelling to me. There's something that is very mass market about it, like something you'd find at a beauty counter at the mall, like at Macy's perhaps. <br />
<br />
I don't really get the tea in the opening, but I do smell the citrusy bergamot and the fruity floral osmanthus that smells like apricot. I wish I smelt more of the tea, since it would have made this perfume less cloying to my nose.<br />
<br />
I can smell hints of jasmine and orange blossom in the heart notes, but the freesia and the rose is what I smell more of. I wish I could smell more of the jasmine and orange blossom and I admittedly don't know what orchids smell like, since I have never smelt an orchid that has a fragrance. I have heard that they have vanilla-like nuances though and I can smell vanilla in this. That is in the base notes too, though.<br />
<br />
The patchouli in Flowerbomb is by far the strongest ingredient in its composition though ans it is what turns this perfume from a soft like to a "meh" for me, since I really don't like patchouli and its strange and sweet earthiness. I smell some of the musk too, but it really takes a back seat to the patchouli.<br />
<br />
As far as its scent and vibe goes, Flowerbomb is like a pink flower and patchouli scented hard candy to me. It smells edible and not completely like a "Flowerbomb." More like a "Flowerbomb" candy. It seems to be a precursor to gourmand fragrances being the most popular fragrance category a few years later and indeed up till now.<br />
<br />
I got 7 hours in total wear time from this perfume and a moderate sillage. I recommend it for spring, fall and winter and for both day and night occasions. I'd also say it's definitely a woman's perfume, despite it not being my cup of tea.<br />
<br />
Altogether, I'd give Flowerbomb by Viktor and Rolf a 5/10. It is as average as average can get for a fragrance for me. It's definitely better than La Vie Est Belle though, which this fragrance is most compared to.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="1965763"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=1965763#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1963539" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;                             <div id="parent2027062" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2027062" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Macleay"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1312640"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1312640.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Macleay" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2027062ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck9x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2027062" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1312640">Macleay</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-01-10">01/10/24 17:36</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I got a rollerball of Flowerbomb a few weeks ago. While I don’t know if I’d purchase a full size, or more precisely a full price full size, I’ve been having fun with my rollerball. I quite like the patchouli hard candy vibe other reviewers have pointed out. It makes me feel like a very pretty, sweet girl with a significant other who dotes on her, a close knit group of friends, and who is always organized and on top of things (but maybe that’s just me projecting my wishes onto the scent). It’s been beloved by so many for a reason. <br />
<br />
I do find it irritating how many reviews seem to be not only calling the scent basic but insulting its wearers. It’s true Flowerbomb has mass market appeal and has been so prevalent in the fragrance world since its release that it now seems not only basic but more than a little passè to many fragheads. But mass market appeal is nothing to scoff at and this is the inevitable journey any highly popular fragrance will pass through. Glossier you, Santal 33, Baccarat rouge 540, Delina etc are starting this transition as well, and soon will be similarly scoffed at. Finally, all that making snide comments about the type of individual that wears this scent or similar others do, is make one look like someone who is into perfume for the exclusivity, rather than sincere appreciation of the art.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/461232">dahrling</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-04-02">04/02/19 00:57</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Unpopular opinion: this smells just as beautiful in the spring/summer as it does in the fall/winter - unlike LVEB this works during all seasons of the year without smelling off and both as a day and a night-time perfume (at least, on my skin when applied with a very LIGHT hand). I don't know if this has been reformulated or not, but the Flowerbomb I know is a very feminine, pretty  fragrance that makes me think of love and joy and all the good simple things in the world. If that makes it "generic" or "boring" or "vanilla" to some, then I'm sorry/not sorry to say that's all I want in my life - it may be a very "safe" fragrance but not all of us are thrill-seekers or sex kittens. I find it innocent and youthful, I don't think it's sexy - at least not Tom Ford or Mugler sexy. This is sweet and cuddly - it's like vanilla ice cream, it may not be everyone's favorite but virtually anyone can have some of it - it's universally appreciated. Vanilla is my favorite ice cream flavor, so maybe this is the perfect fragrance for girls like me. I LOVE it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="1047058"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=1047058#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent670710" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Each note is cooperating with the rest, and nothing feels out of place here. Patchouli is far from my favorite smell. In fact, I used to avoid buying any fragrance if I saw patchouli in the notes. This perfume single-handedly changed my mind. Overall, it's a general people-pleaser while still being complex and interesting and alluring. Sweet, but not too sweet. Feminine, but not juvenile. There's a reason Flowerbomb has been popular for so long.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2073149"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2073149#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2090642" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1945520">lavieenrose1987</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-03-12">03/12/24 16:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>As I’m still new on my fragrance journey, I asked a more knowledgeable acquaintance for recommendations. After listing off a few currently popular choices and some niche fragrances, she then giggled and said, “or, if you want to be basic millennial, you can get Flowerbomb.” Honestly, that right there confirmed that I needed to get my hands on at least a sample. <br />
<br />
While I get that the fragrance industry is just as bad as fast fashion when it comes to a constant stream of new releases and trends, things that are labelled “basic” are popular for a reason. This is a smooth blend of floral and patchouli with some spice on top which gives it a unique kick. I’m not big into super girly and photorealistic florals, so this is a fantastic alternative for someone who wants something feminine with a twist. It’s a fragrance that resonates better with women in my opinion, so if that matters to you, this is your girl.<br />
<br />
If this is what qualifies as “basic”, then call me basic. I notice that Baccarat Rouge 540 is already falling from grace into that category, so don’t worry. Whatever your current it girl fragrance is, it and you will be framed as “basic” soon enough, then "grandma" in a couple decades from now. I look forward to the day that “basic” and “grandma” stop being used as descriptors for scents that have historic popularity.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="2090642"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=2090642#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="1460" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
