<br />
I have tried, truly tried, but I do not understand you.<br />
<br />
In spite of your listed notes, you are no floral. You are Boston fruit slices in a bottle, assorted penny candies liquified, a poor rose swimming in simple syrup.<br />
<br />
Descended you are from Angel, Lolita Lempicka, Euphoria, Coco Mademoiselle and Juicy Couture JC, yet  they manage to be interesting while you twirl your hair and drool. How is it you are so astonishingly popular? I am shocked by it. I wonder if today's girls simply find no discernible difference between flies and men. <br />
<br />
Poor Flowerbomb, a classic of perfumery you are not. You are to Coco Mademoiselle as Giorgio was to Poison. As your simple charms lose their appeal, your formula will cheapened, reduced to a 40 dollar EDT in Wallgreens for our daughters to buy discounted for their "naughties" theme parties, where the teenage girls of 2030 will dress like hipsters, dance to "Sexyback" and say "I can't believe Mom used to wear this!"</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I think this would really suit someone that enjoys very warm, tooth-achingly sweet, strong scents. I prefer something fresher and much, much less sweet.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="689539"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=689539#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent483077" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc483077" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Lybarra118"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/781416"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.781416.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Lybarra118" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Coach/Coach-Floral-Eau-The-Parfum-48115.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.48115.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Coach Floral Eau The Parfum"title="Coach Floral Eau The Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma483077ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd483077" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/781416">Lybarra118</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2014-05-07">05/07/14 10:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Some might hate me for this, but I don't like Flowerbomb. I'm sorry, I know a lot of people love it and I can appreciate that, but I can't stand it. Something about it bothers me and it's not just the fact that I smell it everywhere. I don't like it on myself and I can't stand it on my co-workers. It gives me a headache.<br />
<br />
It's just a dreadful concoction of ingredients, in my opinion; flowers (orchid), patchouli, musk, freesia, and there's even an underlying powdery scent. Not to mention the sweetness. It just doesn't work for me. There are fragrances that smell good on others yet they don't necessarily work on me, but when I smell Flowerbomb on anyone near me, I cringe.<br />
<br />
I've tried to like it, I've tried to force myself. I even still test it at Sephora in hopes something in my nose has changed, but nothing works.<br />
<br />
I don't know, I seem to dislike most popular or "best-selling" perfumes.<br />
<br />
But I will say, Viktor and Rolf have done an excellent marketing job.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="483077"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=483077#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent318498" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc318498" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="annettepe"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/219457"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.219457.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="annettepe" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Memo-Paris/Irish-Leather-18393.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.18393.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Irish Leather"title="Irish Leather"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma318498ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd318498" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/219457">annettepe</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2012-12-27">12/27/12 10:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>i just bought my first Flowerbomb EDP and i love it! to me it does not smell at all like the notes that are listed, nor do i find this extremely florally like the name of the perfume suggests.<br />
<br />
i think this smells gourmand like and very delicious! its very sweet and creamy if thats not weird to say, with strong warm vanilla and faint floral notes. its also a little powdery but in a very comforting way. to me the patchouli is not strong at all even though this got the most votes on the perfume pyramid. just the perfect amount that gives it dimension and depth. its very feminine and i find it quiet sexy and alluring. i think this perfume is suitable for both daily use with a light hand and for the night.<br />
<br />
i kind of got the idea that this fragrance was very screaming and in your face but i personally find it quiet soft but still very distinctive. its such a beautiful scent! it lasts long on my skin which is always a good thing. also i love the bottle, it looks so sophisticated and classy. <br />
<br />
i understand the similarity between this and la vie est belle by Lancome but i find that flowerbomb is a more mature and sophisticated version as i find the la vie est belle more fruity and i somehow tend to associate fruity notes with a younger crowd.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="1460"comment_id="318498"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Viktor-Rolf/Flowerbomb-1460.html?ccid=318498#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="1460" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
